				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Herr Gott, dich loben wir, BWV 16 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>

<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>6 sections
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1726
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Sacred_cantatas&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Sacred cantatas</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Cantatas&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Cantatas</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Religious_works&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Religious works</a></span>; <span class="expandline" title="32 more..."><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_3_voices%2C_mixed_chorus%2C_orchestra&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For 3 voices, mixed chorus, orchestra</a></span>; <h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Herr Gott, dich loben wir
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Lord God, we praise You
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Translations
</th>
<td><span title="ru">Тебя, Бога, хвалим</span>; <span title="ca, es">Herr Gott</span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Authorities
</th>
<td><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.worldcat.org/identities/containsVIAFID/181522066">WorldCat</a>; <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Herr_Gott,_dich_loben_wir,_BWV_16">Wikipedia</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Virtual_International_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Virtual International Authority File">VIAF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://viaf.org/viaf/181522066">181522066</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Johann_Sebastian" title="Category:Bach, Johann Sebastian">Bach, Johann Sebastian</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>BWV 16
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJB 280
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td>C major
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>6 sections:
<ol><li>Chorus: Herr Gott, dich loben wir (C major)
</li><li>Recitative (Bass): So stimmen wir (C major)
</li><li>Aria (Bass) &amp; Chorus: Laßt uns jauchzen, lasst uns freuen (C major)
</li><li>Recitative (Alto): Ach treuer Hort (E minor)
</li><li>Aria (Tenor): Geliebter Jesu, du allein (F major)
</li><li>Chorale: All solch dein Güt wir preisen (A minor)
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1726
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1726-01-01 in Leipzig
</td></tr>

<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>

<td>1852 (BGA)
</td></tr>
